The Board of Directors recommends a vote FOR all nominees, FOR Proposal 2, AGAINST Proposal 3 and AGAINST Proposal 4. 1. To elect three Class II directors to serve for a term of three years or until their respective successors are duly elected and qualified. Nominees: 01 -Antonio Gracias, 02 - James Murdoch, 03 - Kimbal Musk 2. To ratify the appointment of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP as Tesla&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm for the fiscal year ending December 31, 2018. 3. A stockholder proposal to require that the Chair of the Board of Directors be an independent director. 4. A stockholder proposal regarding proxy access.
